Urban Chaos utilises a ground breaking graphics engine which includes 3D volumetric
fog, true wall hugging shadows, atomic matter simulation for real-time physical
modelling of dynamic object collisions and so provides the perfect environment 
for incredible feats of acrobatic skill and total scenery interaction. 
The plot of Urban Chaos is still a closely guarded secret but revolves around end
of the millennium chaos as predictions for Armageddon become more than mere 
fantasy.
Urban Chaos is being developed by Mucky Foot one of the UK's hottest new 
development teams and will be published world-wide by Eidos Interactive.
